FILE: src\App.jsx
================================================================

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import Navbar from './components/Navbar';
import Home from './pages/Home';
import Simulator from './pages/Simulator' ;
import Methodology from './pages/Methodology';
import Validation from './pages/Validation';
import QRCodePage from './pages/QRCodePage';
import Login from './pages/Login';

function App() {
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null); // 'architect' ou 'client'
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState('home');
  const [openProjectsFromHome, setOpenProjectsFromHome] = useState(false);

  if (!user) {
    return <Login onLogin={setUser} />;
  }

  const renderPage = () => {
    switch (currentPage) {
      case 'home':        return <Home setCurrentPage={setCurrentPage} onOpenProjects={() => { setCurrentPage('simulator'); setOpenProjectsFromHome(true); }} user={user} />;
      case 'simulator':   return <Simulator user={user} externalOpenProjects={openProjectsFromHome} setExternalOpenProjects={setOpenProjectsFromHome} />;
      case 'methodology': return <Methodology />;
      case 'validation':  return <Validation />;
      case 'qrcode':      return <QRCodePage />;
      default:            return <Home setCurrentPage={setCurrentPage} />;
    }
  };

  const isSimulator = currentPage === 'simulator';

  return (
    <div style={{ display:'flex', flexDirection:'column', minHeight:'100dvh', background:'#f8fafc' }}>
      <Navbar currentPage={currentPage} setCurrentPage={setCurrentPage} user={user} onLogout={() => setUser(null)} />
      <main style={{ flex:1, display:'flex', flexDirection:'column', overflow: isSimulator ? 'hidden' : 'auto' }}>
        {renderPage()}
      </main>
      {!isSimulator && (
        <footer style={{ background:'white', borderTop:'1px solid #e5e7eb', padding:'1.25rem 2rem', textAlign:'center', color:'#9ca3af', fontSize:'0.85rem' }}>
          Â© 2026 SimArch Durable Â· Plateforme de Simulation d'Architecture Â· Fait avec â¤ï¸ pour la durabilitÃ©
        </footer>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;

FILE: src\components\ProjectManager.jsx

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { FolderOpen, Save, Plus, Trash2, X, Edit2, Check } from 'lucide-react';

/* â”€â”€ LocalStorage helpers â”€â”€ */
const STORAGE_KEY = 'simarch_projects';

export function loadProjects() {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) || []; }
  catch { return []; }
}

export function saveProjects(projects) {
  localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(projects));
}

/* â”€â”€ Modal de gestion de projets â”€â”€ */
export default function ProjectManager({ currentState, onLoad, onClose, user }) {
  const [projects, setProjects]     = useState(loadProjects);
  const [newName, setNewName]       = useState('');
  const [editingId, setEditingId]   = useState(null);
  const [editName, setEditName]     = useState('');
  const [confirmDelete, setConfirmDelete] = useState(null);

  /* â”€â”€ Sauvegarder le projet courant â”€â”€ */
  const handleSave = () => {
    const name = newName.trim();
    if (!name) return;
    const projet = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      name,
      owner: user?.email || 'anonyme',
      role:  user?.role  || 'client',
      date:  new Date().toLocaleDateString('fr-DZ'),
      data:  currentState,
      sharedWith: null // SÃ©curitÃ© : Email du client cible
    };
    const updated = [projet, ...projects];
    setProjects(updated);
    saveProjects(updated);
    setNewName('');
  };

  /* â”€â”€ Ã‰craser / Mettre Ã  jour un projet existant â”€â”€ */
  const handleUpdate = (id) => {
    const updated = projects.map(p =>
      p.id === id ? { ...p, data: currentState, date: new Date().toLocaleDateString('fr-DZ') } : p
    );
    setProjects(updated);
    saveProjects(updated);
  };

  /* â”€â”€ Renommer â”€â”€ */
  const handleRename = (id) => {
    if (!editName.trim()) return;
    const updated = projects.map(p => p.id === id ? { ...p, name: editName.trim() } : p);
    setProjects(updated);
    saveProjects(updated);
    setEditingId(null);
  };

  /* â”€â”€ Supprimer â”€â”€ */
  const handleDelete = (id) => {
    const updated = projects.filter(p => p.id !== id);
    setProjects(updated);
    saveProjects(updated);
    setConfirmDelete(null);
  };

  /* â”€â”€ Partager SÃ©curisÃ© (B2B) â”€â”€ */
  const handleShare = (id) => {
    const targetEmail = window.prompt("ðŸ”’ SÃ‰CURITÃ‰ : Entrez l'email du Promoteur/Organisme de contrÃ´le qui doit valider ce projet :");
    if (!targetEmail || !targetEmail.trim()) return;
    
    const updated = projects.map(p => p.id === id ? { ...p, sharedWith: targetEmail.trim() } : p);
    setProjects(updated);
    saveProjects(updated);
    alert(`âœ… Projet transmis en toute sÃ©curitÃ© Ã  ${targetEmail.trim()}`);
  };

  /* â”€â”€ Charger â”€â”€ */
  const handleLoad = (projet) => {
    onLoad(projet.data);
    onClose();
  };

  const isArchitect = user?.role === 'architect';
  // ðŸ”’ SÃ‰CURITÃ‰ RESTRICTIVE : Le client ne voit QUE les projets expressÃ©ment envoyÃ©s Ã  SON adresse email.
  const visibleProjects = isArchitect ? projects : projects.filter(p => p.sharedWith === user?.email);

  return (
    <div style={{
      position: 'fixed', inset: 0, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',
      display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
      zIndex: 1000, padding: '1rem'
    }}>
      <div style={{
        background: 'white', borderRadius: '1rem', width: '100%', maxWidth: '600px',
        maxHeight: '85vh', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column',
        boxShadow: '0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)'
      }}>
        {/* Header */}
        <div style={{ padding: '1.5rem', borderBottom: '1px solid #e5e7eb', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>
          <div>
            <h2 style={{ fontWeight: 800, fontSize: '1.25rem', margin: 0 }}>ðŸ“ Mes Projets</h2>
            <p style={{ color: '#6b7280', fontSize: '0.8rem', margin: '0.2rem 0 0' }}>
              ConnectÃ© en tant que <strong style={{ color: user?.role === 'architect' ? '#10b981' : '#3b82f6' }}>
                {user?.email}
              </strong>
            </p>
          </div>
          <button onClick={onClose} style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer', color: '#9ca3af', padding: '0.25rem' }}>
            <X size={22} />
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Nouveau projet (Uniquement pour l'Architecte) */}
        {isArchitect && (
          <div style={{ padding: '1.25rem', borderBottom: '1px solid #f3f4f6', background: '#f9fafb' }}>
            <label className="form-label">Sauvegarder la simulation actuelle sous :</label>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '0.5rem', marginTop: '0.4rem' }}>
              <input
                type="text"
                className="form-input"
                value={newName}
                onChange={e => setNewName(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Ex: Villa Bejaia â€” Mur Nord"
                onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSave()}
                style={{ flex: 1 }}
              />
              <button
                className="btn btn-primary"
                onClick={handleSave}
                disabled={!newName.trim()}
                style={{ gap: '0.4rem', whiteSpace: 'nowrap' }}
              >
                <Save size={16}/> Enregistrer
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Liste des projets */}
        <div style={{ overflowY: 'auto', flex: 1, padding: '1rem' }}>
          {visibleProjects.length === 0 ? (
            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '3rem 1rem', color: '#9ca3af' }}>
              <FolderOpen size={40} style={{ opacity: 0.4, marginBottom: '0.75rem' }} />
              <p style={{ fontWeight: 600 }}>Aucun projet disponible</p>
              <p style={{ fontSize: '0.8rem' }}>{isArchitect ? "CrÃ©ez votre premiÃ¨re simulation ci-dessus." : "Aucun projet n'a encore Ã©tÃ© partagÃ© avec vous par l'architecte."}</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '0.625rem' }}>
              {visibleProjects.map(p => (
                <div key={p.id} style={{
                  border: '1px solid #e5e7eb', borderRadius: '0.625rem', padding: '1rem',
                  background: 'white', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '0.75rem',
                  boxShadow: '0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)', transition: 'box-shadow 0.2s'
                }}>
                  {/* IcÃ´ne rÃ´le */}
                  <div style={{
                    width: 38, height: 38, borderRadius: '50%', flexShrink: 0, display: 'flex',
                    alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', fontSize: '1.1rem',
                    background: p.role === 'architect' ? '#ecfdf5' : '#eff6ff'
                  }}>
                    {p.role === 'architect' ? 'ðŸ‘©â€ðŸ’»' : 'ðŸ‘¤'}
                  </div>

                  {/* Nom + mÃ©ta */}
                  <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                    {editingId === p.id ? (
                      <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '0.4rem' }}>
                        <input
                          className="form-input"
                          value={editName}
                          onChange={e => setEditName(e.target.value)}
                          style={{ fontSize: '0.85rem', padding: '0.3rem 0.5rem' }}
                          autoFocus
                          onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleRename(p.id)}
                        />
                        <button onClick={() => handleRename(p.id)} style={{ background: '#10b981', border: 'none', borderRadius: '0.375rem', color: 'white', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '0.3rem 0.5rem' }}>
                          <Check size={14}/>
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div style={{ fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '0.925rem', color: '#1f2937', overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis', whiteSpace: 'nowrap' }}>
                        {p.name}
                      </div>
                    )}
                    <div style={{ fontSize: '0.7rem', color: '#9ca3af', marginTop: '0.15rem' }}>
                      SauvegardÃ© le {p.date} Â· {p.owner} 
                      {p.sharedWith && <span style={{color: '#10b981', fontWeight: 'bold'}}> (âœ… VerrouillÃ© : {p.sharedWith})</span>}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Actions */}
                  <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '0.375rem', flexShrink: 0 }}>
                    <button onClick={() => handleLoad(p)} className="btn btn-primary" style={{ padding: '0.4rem 0.75rem', fontSize: '0.75rem', gap: '0.3rem' }} title="Ouvrir">
                      <FolderOpen size={13}/> {isArchitect ? 'Ouvrir' : 'Consulter (Lecture Seule)'}
                    </button>
                    
                    {isArchitect && (
                      <>
                        {!p.sharedWith ? (
                          <button onClick={() => handleShare(p.id)} className="btn btn-outline" style={{ padding: '0.4rem 0.6rem', color: '#10b981', borderColor: '#a7f3d0' }} title="Partager (SÃ©curisÃ©)">
                            ðŸ“¤ Cibler un destinataire
                          </button>
                        ) : (
                          <button onClick={() => {
                            const updated = projects.map(proj => proj.id === p.id ? { ...proj, sharedWith: null } : proj);
                            setProjects(updated); saveProjects(updated);
                          }} className="btn btn-outline" style={{ padding: '0.4rem 0.6rem', color: '#ef4444', borderColor: '#fecaca' }} title="RÃ©voquer l'accÃ¨s">
                            âŒ Annuler Partage
                          </button>
                        )}
                        <button onClick={() => handleUpdate(p.id)} className="btn btn-outline" style={{ padding: '0.4rem 0.6rem', fontSize: '0.75rem', gap: '0.3rem' }} title="Ã‰craser avec la simulation actuelle">
                          <Save size={13}/>
                        </button>
                        <button onClick={() => { setEditingId(p.id); setEditName(p.name); }} className="btn btn-outline" style={{ padding: '0.4rem 0.6rem' }} title="Renommer">
                          <Edit2 size={13}/>
                        </button>
                        {confirmDelete === p.id ? (
                          <button onClick={() => handleDelete(p.id)} style={{ background: '#ef4444', border: 'none', borderRadius: '0.375rem', color: 'white', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '0.4rem 0.6rem', fontSize: '0.72rem', fontWeight: 700 }}>
                            Confirmer?
                          </button>
                        ) : (
                          <button onClick={() => setConfirmDelete(p.id)} className="btn btn-outline" style={{ padding: '0.4rem 0.6rem', color: '#ef4444', borderColor: '#fecaca' }} title="Supprimer">
                            <Trash2 size={13}/>
                          </button>
                        )}
                      </>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div style={{ padding: '0.875rem 1.25rem', borderTop: '1px solid #f3f4f6', fontSize: '0.72rem', color: '#9ca3af', textAlign: 'center' }}>
          ðŸ’¾ Les projets sont sauvegardÃ©s localement dans votre navigateur (localStorage)
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Leaf, ArrowRight } from 'lucide-react';

export default function Login({ onLogin }) {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setLoading(true); setError('');
    try {
      const res = await fetch('http://localhost/simarch-backend/login.php', {
        method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
        body: JSON.stringify({ email, password })
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.success) onLogin(data.user);
      else setError(data.message || 'Identifiants invalides.');
    } catch {
      if (email === 'archi@simarch.dz')       onLogin({ id:1, email:'archi@simarch.dz',  role:'architect' });
      else if (email === 'client@email.com')  onLogin({ id:2, email:'client@email.com',  role:'client'    });
      else setError('Erreur serveur ou XAMPP non dÃ©tectÃ©. Utilisez les dÃ©mos ci-dessous.');
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div style={{
      display:'flex', justifyContent:'center', alignItems:'center',
      minHeight:'100dvh', padding:'1rem',
      background:`
        radial-gradient(ellipse at 50% 0%,   rgba(0,255,163,0.10) 0%, transparent 55%),
        radial-gradient(ellipse at 100% 100%, rgba(0,212,255,0.06) 0%, transparent 50%),
        #020B18
      `
    }}>

      {/* Card */}
      <div style={{
        width:'100%', maxWidth:420,

        }}>

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Download, Globe, Share2, Smartphone } from 'lucide-react';

function QRImage({ url, size, color }) {
  const fg = color.replace('#', '');
  const src = `https://api.qrserver.com/v1/create-qr-code/?size=${size}x${size}&data=${encodeURIComponent(url)}&color=${fg}&bgcolor=0F172A&qzone=2&format=png`;
  return <img src={src} alt="QR Code" width={size} height={size} style={{ display:'block', borderRadius:'0.5rem' }}/>;
}

const DEPLOY_URL = 'https://simarch-durable.netlify.app';

export default function QRCodePage() {
  const [url, setUrl]     = useState(DEPLOY_URL);
  const [size, setSize]   = useState(256);
  const [color, setColor] = useState('#00FFA3');

  const downloadQR = () => {
    const fg  = color.replace('#', '');
    const src = `https://api.qrserver.com/v1/create-qr-code/?size=${size}x${size}&data=${encodeURIComponent(url)}&color=${fg}&bgcolor=0F172A&qzone=2&format=png`;
    const a   = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = src; a.download = 'simarch-qrcode.png'; a.target = '_blank'; a.click();
  };

function getBioclimaticZone(lat) {
  if (lat > 36.2) return { name: 'Littoral (Zone A)', type: 'humid', wind: ['Brise de mer (Jour)', 'Brise de terre (Nuit)'] };
  if (lat > 34.5) return { name: 'Hauts Plateaux (Zone B)', type: 'semi-arid', wind: ['Vents froids (Nord)', 'Sirocco (Sud)'] };
  if (lat > 32.5) return { name: 'Atlas Saharien (Zone C)', type: 'arid', wind: ['Vents de sable', 'Sirocco dominant'] };
  return { name: 'Sahara (Zone D)', type: 'hyper-arid', wind: ['Sirocco intense (Chehili)', 'Brise thermique dÃ©sertique'] };
}

const STANDARD_U = 2.5;

/* â”€â”€ Intelligent recommendation engine â”€â”€ */
function getRecommendations({ uValue, flj, energySavings, win, layers, co2Reduction, location }) {
  const recs = [];
  const zone = getBioclimaticZone(location.lat);

  // recommendations par zone bioclimatique algÃ©rienne
  if (zone.type === 'humid') {
    recs.push({
      type: 'warning', icon: 'ðŸŒŠ',
      title: `StratÃ©gie Littorale : ${zone.name}`,
      text: `Exploitez la ${zone.wind[0]} pour la ventilation naturelle nocturne. MatÃ©riaux : BÃ©ton armÃ© banchÃ© ou Brique avec enduit ciment hydrophobe.`,
      action: 'Favoriser la ventilation traversante'
    });
  } else if (zone.type === 'hyper-arid' || zone.type === 'arid') {
    recs.push({
      type: 'warning', icon: 'ðŸœï¸',
      title: `StratÃ©gie Saharienne : ${zone.name}`,
      text: `Protection contre le ${zone.wind[0]} requise. Utilisez une forte inertie (Pierre ou Terre cuite pleine) pour absorber la chaleur la journÃ©e.`,
      action: 'Utiliser des parois Ã  forte inertie thermique'
    });
  } else {
    recs.push({
      type: 'warning', icon: 'â›°ï¸',
      title: `StratÃ©gie Hauts Plateaux : ${zone.name}`,
      text: `Isolation renforcÃ©e obligatoire contre les ${zone.wind[0]}. Attention au ${zone.wind[1]} (Chehili) en Ã©tÃ© : fermez les baies au Sud.`,
      action: 'Prioriser l\'Isolation par l\'ExtÃ©rieur (ITE)'
    });
  }

  if (uValue > 1.5) {
    recs.push({
      type: 'danger', icon: 'ðŸ”¥',
      title: 'Isolation insuffisante',
      text: `Valeur-U (${uValue.toFixed(2)}) trop Ã©levÃ©e. Danger de dÃ©perdition majeure. Ajoutez 10cm d'Isolant EPS ou Laine de Roche.`,
      action: 'Ajouter un isolant (min 10cm)'
    });
  } else if (uValue > 0.8) {
    recs.push({
      type: 'warning', icon: 'âš ï¸',
      title: 'Performance moyenne',
      text: `Valeur-U = ${uValue.toFixed(2)}. Correct pour le bÃ¢timent standard, mais insuffisant pour le confort passif.`,
      action: 'Optimiser l\'Ã©paisseur d\'isolant'
    });
  } else {
    recs.push({
      type: 'success', icon: 'âœ…',
      title: 'Excellente Isolation',
      text: `Valeur-U = ${uValue.toFixed(2)}. Paroi trÃ¨s performante conforme aux standards internationaux.`,
      action: null
    });
  }

  if (flj < 2) {
    recs.push({
      type: 'warning', icon: 'ðŸ’¡',
      title: 'LumiÃ¨re Naturelle Faible',
      text: `FLJ = ${flj.toFixed(1)}%. Risque d'inconfort visuel. Augmentez la surface vitrÃ©e ou utilisez des vitrages Ã  haute transmission (TL).`,
      action: 'Agrandir la fenÃªtre ou modifier TL'
    });
  }

  if (win.shadingFactor > 0.5 && (win.orientation === 'Sud' || win.orientation === 'Ouest')) {
    recs.push({
      type: 'danger', icon: 'ðŸŒ¡ï¸',
      title: 'Risque Surchauffe (WWR)',
      text: `Orientation ${win.orientation} vulnÃ©rable. Ajoutez des protections solaires (Brise-soleil, volets) pour rÃ©duire l'apport direct.`,
      action: 'Installer des brise-soleil fixes ou mobiles'
    });
  }

  if (co2Reduction < 15) {
    recs.push({
      type: 'warning', icon: 'ðŸŒ¿',
      title: 'Bilan Carbone Faible',
      text: `RÃ©duction COâ‚‚ faible (${co2Reduction.toFixed(0)} kg/an). IntÃ©grez des matÃ©riaux comme le Bois ou la Terre Cuite pour un meilleur bilan.`,
      action: 'Modifier la composition vers des matÃ©riaux durables'
    });
  }

  return recs;
}

/* â”€â”€ PDF Generator (text-based, no screenshot) â”€â”€ */
function generatePDF({ uValue, rValue, energySavings, co2Reduction, flj, gainEte, perteHiver, layers, win, climate, location, recommendations }) {
  const pdf    = new jsPDF('p', 'mm', 'a4');
  const W      = pdf.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const margin = 20;
  let y        = margin;

  const addLine = (txt, sz = 11, style = 'normal', color = [30, 30, 30]) => {
    pdf.setFontSize(sz);
    pdf.setFont('helvetica', style);
    pdf.setTextColor(...color);
    pdf.text(txt, margin, y);
    y += sz * 0.7;
  };

  const addSep = (h = 6) => { y += h; };

  const addPara = (txt, sz = 10) => {
    pdf.setFontSize(sz);
    pdf.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    pdf.setTextColor(60, 60, 60);
    const lines = pdf.splitTextToSize(txt, W - margin * 2);
    lines.forEach(line => {
      if (y > 275) { pdf.addPage(); y = margin; }
      pdf.text(line, margin, y);
      y += 5;
    });
    y += 2;
  };

  // Header Decor
  pdf.setFillColor(16, 185, 129);
  pdf.rect(0, 0, W, 25, 'F');
  pdf.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  pdf.setFontSize(18);
  pdf.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  pdf.text('RAPPORT DE PERFORMANCE BIOCLIMATIQUE', margin, 16);
  y = 35;

  const zone = getBioclimaticZone(location.lat);

  // 1. SpÃ©cifications Techniques
  addLine('1. SpÃ©cifications Techniques des MatÃ©riaux', 13, 'bold', [16, 140, 100]);
  addPara("Le choix du BÃ©ton ArmÃ© est complÃ©tÃ© par ses caractÃ©ristiques de densitÃ© et de conductivitÃ© thermique (\u03bb). Pour les zones arides, nous prÃ©conisons le BÃ©ton de Terre pour son inertie thermique Ã©levÃ©e, permettant de rÃ©guler naturellement les pics de chaleur.");
  
  addLine('Composition de la paroi simulÃ©e :', 11, 'bold');
  layers.forEach((l, i) => {
    const m = MATERIALS.find(mat => mat.id === l.materialId);
    addLine(`   - Couche ${i+1} : ${m.name} (${l.thickness*100} cm) | \u03bb = ${m.lambda} W/mK`);
  });
  y += 5;

  // 2. Analyse Bioclimatique
  addLine('2. Analyse Bioclimatique par RÃ©gion', 13, 'bold', [16, 140, 100]);
  if (zone.type === 'humid') {
    addPara("Zone Littorale : PrioritÃ© Ã  la gestion de l'humiditÃ© et Ã  l'exploitation de la brise de mer pour le rafraÃ®chissement passif. L'utilisation de matÃ©riaux rÃ©sistants Ã  la corrosion saline est recommandÃ©e.");
  } else {
    addPara("Zone Aride / Hauts Plateaux : Recommandation de matÃ©riaux Ã  forte inertie et rÃ©duction des surfaces vitrÃ©es exposÃ©es au Sirocco (vent chaud de sable). L'isolation par l'extÃ©rieur est prioritaire.");
  }
  y += 5;

  // 3. Dynamique des Vents
  addLine('3. Dynamique des Vents et Ventilation', 13, 'bold', [16, 140, 100]);
  addPara(`L'outil intÃ¨gre l'impact de la Dynamique des Vents locaux : ${zone.wind.join(' et ')}. L'architecte reÃ§oit des conseils sur l'orientation des ouvertures pour favoriser la ventilation transversale tout en se protÃ©geant des vents froids du Nord en hiver.`);
  y += 5;

  // 4. Analyse des Ouvertures et Uw
  addLine('4. Analyse des Ouvertures et Coefficient Uw', 13, 'bold', [16, 140, 100]);
  addPara("Le Coefficient Uw reprÃ©sente la capacitÃ© de la paroi vitrÃ©e Ã  laisser passer la chaleur. Il combine la performance thermique du vitrage (Ug) et celle du chÃ¢ssis (Uf). C'est l'indicateur clÃ© pour Ã©valuer les pertes hivernales et les gains excessifs en Ã©tÃ©.");
  addLine(`â€¢ Uw actuel de votre projet : ${win.uWindow} W/m\u00b2K`, 11, 'bold');
  if (zone.type === 'humid') {
    addPara("ðŸ’¡ RECOMMANDATION : En Zone Littorale, nous prÃ©conisons un Uw < 2.5 W/m\u00b2K pour limiter l'impact de l'humiditÃ© et rÃ©duire la charge de climatisation.");
  } else {
    addPara("ðŸ’¡ RECOMMANDATION : En Zone Aride, privilÃ©giez des protections solaires mobiles pour compenser le rayonnement direct intense.");
  }
  y += 5;

  // 5. RÃ©sultats NumÃ©riques
  addLine('5. Indicateurs de Performance Globale', 13, 'bold', [16, 140, 100]);
  addLine(`â€¢ Valeur-U mur : ${uValue.toFixed(3)} W/m\u00b2K`, 11);
  addLine(`â€¢ Ã‰clairage Naturel (FLJ) : ${flj.toFixed(1)} %`, 11);
  addLine(`â€¢ RÃ©duction CO2 estimÃ©e : ${co2Reduction.toFixed(1)} kg/an`, 11);
  y += 10;

  // 6. Assistant Intelligent
  addLine('6. Conseils de l\'Assistant Intelligent', 13, 'bold', [200, 30, 30]);
  addSep(2);
  recommendations.forEach((r, i) => {
    const color = r.type === 'danger' ? [200,30,30] : r.type === 'warning' ? [180,120,0] : [16,140,100];
    addLine(`${i+1}. ${r.icon} ${r.title}`, 10, 'bold', color);
    addPara(`   ${r.text}`, 9);
    if (r.action) {
       addLine(`   -> Action : ${r.action}`, 9, 'italic', [16, 140, 100]);
       y += 2;
    }
    y += 2;
  });

  // Footer
  pdf.setFontSize(8);
  pdf.setTextColor(150, 150, 150);
  pdf.text('Â© SimArch Durable â€” Analyse paramÃ©trique certifiÃ©e ' + new Date().getFullYear(), W/2, 285, {align:'center'});

  pdf.save('SimArch_Rapport_Expert.pdf');
}

/* â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ COMPONENT â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ */
export default function Simulator({ user, externalOpenProjects, setExternalOpenProjects }) {
  const isArchitect = user?.role === 'architect';
  const dashboardRef = useRef(null);
  const [showProjects, setShowProjects] = useState(false);
  const [step, setStep] = useState(1);

  // Ã‰couter si l'ordre d'ouvrir est envoyÃ© depuis Home
  useEffect(() => {
    if (externalOpenProjects) {
      setShowProjects(true);
      if (setExternalOpenProjects) setExternalOpenProjects(false);
    }
  }, [externalOpenProjects, setExternalOpenProjects]);

  const [location, setLocation] = useState({ lat: 36.9, lng: 7.766 });
  const [climate,  setClimate]  = useState({ temp: 24, humidity: 65, sunHours: 8 });

  const [layers, setLayers] = useState([
    { id: 'l1', materialId: 'brick_hollow', thickness: 0.20 },
    { id: 'l2', materialId: 'plaster',      thickness: 0.02 },
  ]);

  const [win, setWin] = useState({
    width: 1.5, height: 1.2, orientation: 'Sud',
    shadingFactor: 0.5, uWindow: 1.3, roomArea: 15, tl: 0.7,
  });

  /* Thermal */
  const rValue = useMemo(() => {
    let r = 0.17;
    layers.forEach(l => {
      const m = MATERIALS.find(m => m.id === l.materialId);
      if (m) r += l.thickness / m.lambda;
    });
    return r;
  }, [layers]);

  const uValue      = 1 / rValue;
  const energySavings = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, ((STANDARD_U - uValue) / STANDARD_U) * 100));
  const co2Reduction  = energySavings * 1.2;
  const windowArea  = win.width * win.height;
  const ORIENTATION_COEFFS = { 'Sud': 0.75, 'Ouest': 1.0, 'Est': 0.85, 'Nord': 0.25 };
  const irradiance  = 850 * (ORIENTATION_COEFFS[win.orientation] || 0.75);
  const gainEte     = windowArea * irradiance * win.shadingFactor * win.tl;
  const dtHiver     = 20 - Math.max(0, climate.temp - 10);
  const perteHiver  = windowArea * win.uWindow * dtHiver;
  const flj         = (windowArea * win.tl * 0.5 * 100) / win.roomArea;

  const recommendations = useMemo(() =>
    getRecommendations({ uValue, flj, energySavings, win, layers, co2Reduction, location }),
    [uValue, flj, energySavings, win, layers, co2Reduction, location]
  );

  /* Charts */
  const gradientData = useMemo(() => {
    const labels = ['Ext.']; const data = [0]; let drop = 0;
    layers.forEach(l => {
      const m = MATERIALS.find(m => m.id === l.materialId);
      if (m) {
        drop += ((l.thickness / m.lambda) / rValue) * 100;
        labels.push(m.name); data.push(drop);
      }
    });
    labels.push('Int.'); data.push(100);
    return { labels, datasets: [{ label:'Chute Temp (%)', data, borderColor:'#10b981', backgroundColor:'#10b98115', fill:true, tension:0.3 }] };
  }, [layers, rValue]);

  const comparisonData = {
    labels: ['Standard (rÃ©f.)', 'Votre Solution'],
    datasets: [
      { label:'Valeur-U (W/mÂ²K)',  data:[STANDARD_U, uValue],        backgroundColor:['#fca5a5','#6ee7b7'] },
    ]
  };

  /* Handlers */
  const addLayer    = () => setLayers([...layers, { id:`l${Date.now()}`, materialId:'insulation', thickness:0.1 }]);
  const removeLayer = id => setLayers(layers.filter(l => l.id !== id));
  const updateLayer = (id, key, val) => setLayers(layers.map(l => l.id === id ? {...l, [key]:val} : l));

  const LocationPicker = () => {
    useMapEvents({ click(e) {
      setLocation({ lat: e.latlng.lat, lng: e.latlng.lng });
      setClimate({
        temp:     Math.round(20 + (36 - e.latlng.lat) * 2),
        humidity: Math.round(65 - (36 - e.latlng.lat) * 5),
        sunHours: Math.round(8  + (36 - e.latlng.lat) * 0.5),
      });
    }});
    return <Marker position={[location.lat, location.lng]} />;
  };

  const handleExportPDF = () => generatePDF({
    uValue, rValue, energySavings, co2Reduction, flj, gainEte, perteHiver,
    layers, win, climate, location, recommendations
  });

  /* â”€â”€ Project state snapshot â”€â”€ */
  const currentState = { location, climate, layers, win };

  const handleLoadProject = ({ location: loc, climate: cli, layers: lay, win: w }) => {
    setLocation(loc);
    setClimate(cli);
    setLayers(lay);
    setWin(w);
  };

  /* â”€â”€ Colors for rec badge â”€â”€ */
  // Dark-mode rec styles (bg:border:color)
  const parseStyle = type => {
    const map = {
      danger:  { bg:'rgba(255,61,107,0.08)',  border:'rgba(255,61,107,0.25)',  color:'#FF3D6B' },
      warning: { bg:'rgba(255,184,0,0.08)',   border:'rgba(255,184,0,0.25)',   color:'#FFB800' },
      success: { bg:'rgba(0,255,163,0.06)',   border:'rgba(0,255,163,0.25)',   color:'#00FFA3' },
    };
    return map[type] || map.warning;
  };

  /* â”€â”€ Step Nav helpers â”€â”€ */
  const zone = getBioclimaticZone(location.lat);
  const STEPS = [
    { n:1, label:'GÃ©oclimat',  icon:'ðŸ—ºï¸' },
    { n:2, label:'Paroi',      icon:'ðŸ§±' },
    { n:3, label:'Baies',      icon:'ðŸªŸ' },
    { n:4, label:'Dashboard',  icon:'ðŸ“Š' },
  ];

  return (
    <div style={{ minHeight:'calc(100dvh - 62px)', display:'flex', flexDirection:'column', background:'#020B18', overflow:'hidden', position:'relative' }}>

      <div style={{

        display:'flex', justifyContent:'center', alignItems:'center', gap:'2rem',

        flexWrap: 'wrap'

                transition:'all 0.3s ease'

            >
              <div style={{
                width:32, height:32, borderRadius:'50%',
                background: step >= s.n ? 'rgba(0,255,163,0.1)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)',
                border: `1px solid ${step >= s.n ? '#00FFA3' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}`,
                display:'flex', alignItems:'center', justifyContent:'center',
                color: step >= s.n ? '#00FFA3' : '#94A3B8',
                boxShadow: step === s.n ? '0 0 15px rgba(0,255,163,0.3)' : 'none',

            {i < STEPS.length - 1 && (
              <div style={{ flex:1, maxWidth:60, height:2, background: s.n < step ? '#00FFA3' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)', transition:'background 0.3s ease' }}/>

      {/* â”€â”€ CONTENT AREA â”€â”€ */}

        {/* STEP 1: GÃ‰OCLIMAT */}

                    Vents dominants : {zone.wind.join(' / ')}
                  </div>

                <div style={{ display:'grid', gridTemplateColumns:'1fr', gap:'0.75rem' }}>

                    return (

                        <div style={{ display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:'0.75rem', marginBottom:'0.75rem' }}>

                    <div style={{ fontSize:'2.5rem', fontWeight:900, color: uValue<=STANDARD_U ? '#00FFA3' : '#FF3D6B', lineHeight:1, fontFamily:"'JetBrains Mono',monospace" }}>{uValue.toFixed(2)}</div>

                      data={{labels:['Ã‰conomies','Pertes'],datasets:[{data:[energySavings,100-energySavings],backgroundColor:['#00FFA3','rgba(255,255,255,0.05)'],borderColor:['rgba(0,255,163,0.5)','rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'],borderWidth:1}]}}

                  </div>
                </div>
              </NeonCard>

              <NeonCard style={{ padding:'1.5rem' }}>
                <h3 style={{ fontSize:'1rem', color:'#F1F5F9', fontWeight:700, marginBottom:'1.5rem', display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:'0.5rem' }}>
                  <Zap size={16} color="#BD93F9"/> Gradient Thermique â€” Courbe NÃ©on
                </h3>

                  <Line data={{...gradientData, datasets:[{...gradientData.datasets[0], borderColor:'#00FFA3', backgroundColor:'rgba(0,255,163,0.05)', pointBackgroundColor:'#00FFA3', pointRadius:5, borderWidth:3, tension:0.4}]}} options={{

                  }}/>

                {recommendations.map((r,i)=>{

                  return (

                        <div style={{ fontSize:'0.75rem', fontWeight:700, color:s.color, background:'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)', padding:'0.4rem 0.75rem', borderRadius:'0.5rem', display:'inline-block', border:`1px solid ${s.border}` }}>
                          â†’ {r.action}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </NeonCard>

          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* â”€â”€ Project Manager Modal â”€â”€ */}
      {showProjects && (
        <ProjectManager
          currentState={currentState}
          onLoad={handleLoadProject}
          onClose={() => setShowProjects(false)}
          user={user}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

================================================================
FILE: backend\login.php
================================================================

 <?php
// backend/login.php
header("Access-Control-Allow-Origin: *");
header("Access-Control-Allow-Headers: Content-Type");
header("Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8");

// Options database connection pour XAMPP local
$servername = "localhost";
$username = "root";
$password = "";
$dbname = "simarch_db";

// Connexion mysqli (Port 3307)
$conn = new mysqli($servername, $username, $password, $dbname, 3307);

if ($conn->connect_error) {
    die(json_encode(["success" => false, "message" => "Erreur de connexion MySQL : " . $conn->connect_error]));
}

// RÃ©cupÃ©ration du body JSON de l'application React
$data = json_decode(file_get_contents("php://input"));

if(isset($data->email) && isset($data->password)) {
    $email = $conn->real_escape_string($data->email);
    $pass = $conn->real_escape_string($data->password);

    // RequÃªte pour vÃ©rifier les identifiants
    $sql = "SELECT id, email, role FROM users WHERE email='$email' AND password='$pass'";
    $result = $conn->query($sql);

    // RÃ©sultat
    if ($result->num_rows > 0) {
        $row = $result->fetch_assoc();
        echo json_encode(["success" => true, "user" => $row]);
    } else {
        echo json_encode(["success" => false, "message" => "Identifiants ou mot de passe incorrects."]);
    }
} else {
    echo json_encode(["success" => false, "message" => "Veuillez remplir email et mot de passe."]);
}

$conn->close();
?>
